D Type Automatic Folding Car Door

=20
=09

D - Type Automatic Folding Car Door

=20
=20
=20 =20 =20 =20 =20

D TYPE AUTOMATIC FOLDING CABINET= DOOR FEATURES

  • Easy and practical assembly can be made.
  • It operates with supply voltage 220 V AC and LIR voltage.
  • Length, size and speed parameters can be adjusted.
  • Electronic control can be made.
  • There is a jam control.
  • It has battery and photocell output.
  • It works with a 24 V DC brushed motor.
  • Stainless or Rail painted option
